### [74] [CCD-Bench: Probing Cultural Conflict in Large Language Model Decision-Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.03553)
*Hasibur Rahman,Hanan Salam*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在跨文化价值冲突情境下的决策能力未得到充分研究。本研究提出了CCD-Bench，一个包含2182个跨文化价值冲突困境的基准测试，涵盖七个领域。研究评估了17个LLMs，发现模型倾向于偏爱北欧和日耳曼欧洲的文化价值，而东欧和中东北非的选项则代表性不足。尽管模型在理由中常提及多个 GLOBE 维度，但这种多元化是肤浅的，很少基于进取心或性别平等原则。研究还发现模型决策更多地受其开发者 lineage 影响，而非地理位置。这表明当前的对齐（alignment）策略倾向于一种“共识导向”的世界观，未能充分处理需要权力协商、权利论证或性别视角分析的情境。CCD-Bench 旨在推动评估超越孤立的偏见检测，转向多元化决策，并强调需要更深入地融合不同世界观的对齐策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLMs）评估基准主要关注文化知识、价值预测或单一偏见检测，未能充分考察LLMs在面对合法存在的、且相互冲突的文化价值体系时的决策能力。然而，LLMs日益被应用于人际和社会决策，因此理解其在跨文化价值冲突情境下的行为至关重要。本研究旨在填补这一空白，通过开发一个专门用于评估LLMs在跨文化价值冲突下决策能力的基准测试，来揭示当前LLMs在处理复杂、多元文化情境时的局限性，并为未来LLMs的对齐策略提供指导。

Method: 本研究提出了CCD-Bench，一个包含2182个开放式困境的基准测试，用于评估LLMs在跨文化价值冲突下的决策能力。这些困境涵盖七个领域，每个困境都配有十个匿名选项，分别对应GLOBE文化集群中的十个文化维度。为了减少排序效应的影响，困境以分层拉丁方设计呈现。研究评估了17个非推理（non-reasoning）的LLMs。评估指标包括选项的选择频率、理由的多元化程度（通过提及GLOBE维度的数量衡量）以及对特定文化维度的依赖性。此外，研究还使用Cramer

Result: 研究评估了17个LLMs在CCD-Bench基准测试上的表现。结果显示，模型在决策时不成比例地偏爱“北欧”（Nordic Europe，平均占比20.2%）和“日耳曼欧洲”（Germanic Europe，占比12.4%）的文化选项，而“东欧”（Eastern Europe）和“中东北非”（Middle East and North Africa）的选项则代表性不足（占比5.6%至5.8%）。尽管87.9%的LLM生成的理由提及了多个GLOBE维度，但这种多元化是表面化的。模型倾向于组合“未来导向”（Future Orientation）和“绩效导向”（Performance Orientation），而很少基于“进取心”（Assertiveness）或“性别平等”（Gender Egalitarianism）维度进行决策（两者占比均低于3%）。排序效应对模型决策的影响微乎其微（Cramer

Conclusion: 本研究通过CCD-Bench基准测试揭示了当前大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理跨文化价值冲突时存在的显著局限性。研究发现，LLMs倾向于偏爱某些文化区域的价值，并且在理由生成中虽然看似多元化，实则缺乏对特定文化维度（如进取心和性别平等）的实质性考量。模型决策模式更多地反映了其开发者 lineage，而非地理文化集群的差异。这表明当前的LLM对齐（alignment）策略可能无意中推广了一种“共识导向”的世界观，这种世界观在面对需要权力协商、权利论证或性别意识的复杂情境时显得不足。CCD-Bench 的提出，将LLMs的评估从孤立的偏见检测，转向了更贴近现实的多元化决策场景。研究强调，未来的LLM对齐策略需要进行创新，以更深刻、实质性地融合和代表不同的世界观，从而使LLMs能够在更广泛的跨文化交际和决策场景中发挥更公平、更有效的作用。研究的局限性在于模型评估主要基于文本生成，未来的工作可以探索更深层次的因果推理和对模型内部机制的理解，并进一步扩展基准测试的文化覆盖范围和困境的复杂性。

Abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) are increasingly implicated in interpersonal and societal decision-making, their ability to navigate explicit conflicts between legitimately different cultural value systems remains largely unexamined. Existing benchmarks predominantly target cultural knowledge (CulturalBench), value prediction (WorldValuesBench), or single-axis bias diagnostics (CDEval); none evaluate how LLMs adjudicate when multiple culturally grounded values directly clash. We address this gap with CCD-Bench, a benchmark that assesses LLM decision-making under cross-cultural value conflict. CCD-Bench comprises 2,182 open-ended dilemmas spanning seven domains, each paired with ten anonymized response options corresponding to the ten GLOBE cultural clusters. These dilemmas are presented using a stratified Latin square to mitigate ordering effects. We evaluate 17 non-reasoning LLMs. Models disproportionately prefer Nordic Europe (mean 20.2 percent) and Germanic Europe (12.4 percent), while options for Eastern Europe and the Middle East and North Africa are underrepresented (5.6 to 5.8 percent). Although 87.9 percent of rationales reference multiple GLOBE dimensions, this pluralism is superficial: models recombine Future Orientation and Performance Orientation, and rarely ground choices in Assertiveness or Gender Egalitarianism (both under 3 percent). Ordering effects are negligible (Cramer's V less than 0.10), and symmetrized KL divergence shows clustering by developer lineage rather than geography. These patterns suggest that current alignment pipelines promote a consensus-oriented worldview that underserves scenarios demanding power negotiation, rights-based reasoning, or gender-aware analysis. CCD-Bench shifts evaluation beyond isolated bias detection toward pluralistic decision making and highlights the need for alignment strategies that substantively engage diverse worldviews.

### [75] [A Critical Review of the Need for Knowledge-Centric Evaluation of Quranic Recitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.12858)
*Mohammed Hilal Al-Kharusi,Khizar Hayat,Khalil Bader Al Ruqeishi,Haroon Rashid Lone*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有的自动语音识别（ASR）系统在评估古兰经诵读（Tajweed）方面存在不足，因为它们侧重于词语识别而非定性声学评估，并存在数据集偏见和反馈有限的问题。作者提出应转向基于规则的计算框架，利用古兰经文本的稳定性和Tajweed规则，侧重于发音规则（Makhraj）而非有偏见的数据。未来的方法应结合语言学专业知识和先进的音频处理技术，以创建可靠、公平且具有教育意义的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的数字时代为学习古兰经诵读（Tajweed）提供了机会，但现有的自动评估系统在教育有效性方面并未获得广泛认可。这主要是因为现有系统基于自动语音识别（ASR）技术，过度关注词语识别，而忽略了定性声学评估。这些系统存在依赖有偏见的数据集、人口统计学差异以及无法提供有价值的反馈等局限性。因此，有必要解决这一差距，以开发更有效的评估工具。

Method: 该研究通过文献综述，对过去二十年内关于古兰经诵读评估的学术研究、数字平台和商业工具进行了深入分析。重点考察了现有基于ASR的方法的局限性，并提出了转向基于规则的计算框架的建议。该框架将利用古兰经文本的固定性和Tajweed的明确规则，侧重于基于规则的声学建模，特别是发音点（Makhraj）和标准发音原则，而不是依赖于有偏差的数据。

Result: 文献综述发现，现有的基于ASR的评估方法在评估古兰经诵读方面存在根本性缺陷，主要表现在对词语识别的过度依赖，以及由此带来的数据集偏见、人口统计学差异和反馈不足等问题。这些方法未能提供有效的、可供学习者改进的反馈。

Conclusion: 当前的自动古兰经诵读评估方法存在显著局限性，无法满足教育需求。作者主张采用一种新的范式，即基于规则的计算框架，该框架应利用古兰经文本的稳定性和Tajweed规则，并结合语言学知识和先进的音频处理技术。未来的评估工具应更加可靠、公平，并具有真正的教育价值，能够为全球学习者提供有效的帮助。

Abstract: The art and science of Quranic recitation (Tajweed), a discipline governed by meticulous phonetic, rhythmic, and theological principles, confronts substantial educational challenges in today's digital age. Although modern technology offers unparalleled opportunities for learning, existing automated systems for evaluating recitation have struggled to gain broad acceptance or demonstrate educational effectiveness. This literature review examines this crucial disparity, offering a thorough analysis of scholarly research, digital platforms, and commercial tools developed over the past twenty years. Our analysis uncovers a fundamental flaw in current approaches that adapt Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) systems, which emphasize word identification over qualitative acoustic evaluation. These systems suffer from limitations such as reliance on biased datasets, demographic disparities, and an inability to deliver meaningful feedback for improvement. Challenging these data-centric methodologies, we advocate for a paradigm shift toward a knowledge-based computational framework. By leveraging the unchanging nature of the Quranic text and the well-defined rules of Tajweed, we propose that an effective evaluation system should be built upon rule-based acoustic modeling centered on canonical pronunciation principles and articulation points (Makhraj), rather than depending on statistical patterns derived from flawed or biased data. The review concludes that the future of automated Quranic recitation assessment lies in hybrid systems that combine linguistic expertise with advanced audio processing. Such an approach paves the way for developing reliable, fair, and pedagogically effective tools that can authentically assist learners across the globe.

### [76] [FlowMM: Cross-Modal Information Flow Guided KV Cache Merging for Efficient Multimodal Context Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.05534)
*Kunxi Li,Yufan Xiong,Zhonghua Jiang,Yiyun Zhou,Zhaode Wang,Chengfei Lv,Shengyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: FlowMM通过跨模态信息流和敏感度自适应匹配机制，实现了高效且高质量的多模态KV缓存合并，显著减少内存占用和解码延迟，同时保持任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的KV缓存逐出策略（如基于注意力分数丢弃KV对）会降低生成质量，导致上下文丢失或幻觉。近期的KV合并策略虽然有所改进，但在多模态场景下，跨模态分布偏差和注意力偏差限制了其有效性。因此，需要一种能够有效处理多模态信息的KV缓存合并方法，以解决现有方法的局限性。

Method: FlowMM框架利用跨模态信息流来指导多模态KV缓存的合并。它采用动态的、特定于层的合并策略，以捕捉特定模态的模式并保持上下文完整性。此外，FlowMM引入了一个敏感度自适应的令牌匹配机制，该机制结合了令牌相似度和任务关键敏感度，优先合并低风险令牌，同时保护高敏感度令牌。

Result: FlowMM在多种领先的多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）上的广泛实验表明，该方法能够将KV缓存内存减少80%至95%，并将解码延迟降低1.3-1.8倍。在实现显著效率提升的同时，FlowMM保持了具有竞争力的任务性能。

Conclusion: FlowMM提供了一种新颖有效的多模态KV缓存合并框架，通过跨模态信息流和敏感度自适应匹配机制，成功解决了现有方法的不足。该研究不仅在内存占用和解码速度上取得了显著的效率提升，而且在任务性能上保持了竞争力，为多模态大语言模型的高效推理提供了有价值的解决方案。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的跨模态交互模式和更精细的敏感度评估方法。

Abstract: Traditional KV cache eviction strategies, which discard less critical KV-pairs based on attention scores, often degrade generation quality, causing context loss or hallucinations. Recent efforts shift toward KV merging, merging eviction tokens with retention tokens based on similarity. However, in multimodal scenarios, distributional biases across modality tokens and attentional biases in cross-modal interactions limit its effectiveness. This work introduces FlowMM, an adaptive framework for cross-modal information flow-guided multimodal KV cache merging. FlowMM leverages cross-modal information flow to dynamically apply layer-specific merging strategies, capturing modality-specific patterns while preserving contextual integrity. Furthermore, we introduce a sensitivity-adaptive token matching mechanism that jointly evaluates token similarity and task-critical sensitivity, merging low-risk tokens while safeguarding high-sensitivity ones. Extensive experiments across diverse leading MLLMs show that FlowMM reduces KV cache memory by 80% to 95% and decoding latency by 1.3-1.8x, while maintaining competitive task performance.

</details>


### [77] [Retrieval-Augmented Generation in Medicine: A Scoping Review of Technical Implementations, Clinical Applications, and Ethical Considerations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.05901)
*Rui Yang,Matthew Yu Heng Wong,Huitao Li,Xin Li,Wentao Zhu,Jingchi Liao,Kunyu Yu,Jonathan Chong Kai Liew,Weihao Xuan,Yingjian Chen,Yuhe Ke,Jasmine Chiat Ling Ong,Douglas Teodoro,Chuan Hong,Daniel Shi Wei Ting,Nan Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文综述了检索增强生成（RAG）技术在医学领域的应用。研究发现，当前医学RAG研究主要使用公开数据，检索模型以英语为主，生成模型通用性强。评估方法上，自动评估关注生成质量和任务表现，人工评估关注准确性、完整性、相关性和流畅性，但对偏见和安全的关注不足。RAG主要应用于问答、报告生成、文本摘要和信息提取。研究认为，医学RAG仍处于早期阶段，需在临床验证、跨语言适应和低资源场景支持方面取得进展，以实现可信赖和负责任的全球应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着医学知识的快速增长和临床实践复杂性的增加，大型语言模型（LLMs）在医学领域展现出潜力，但其固有的局限性限制了临床应用。检索增强生成（RAG）技术被认为是提高LLMs在医学领域应用能力的一种有前景的方法。因此，本研究旨在全面回顾和分析RAG在医学领域的应用现状，以期为未来的研究和发展提供指导。

Method: 本研究通过对医学领域RAG应用的文献进行系统性回顾。分析了研究中使用的主要数据类型（公开 vs. 私有）、检索方法（嵌入模型）、生成模型（通用 LLMs vs. 医学 LLMs）、评估方法（自动 vs. 人工，评估维度）以及具体的应用场景。最后，总结了当前医学RAG的整体发展阶段，并指出了未来需要改进的方向。

Result: 研究发现，医学RAG研究主要依赖公开可用数据，对私有数据的应用有限。检索方面，研究多采用以英语为中心的嵌入模型。生成模型方面，大多数研究使用通用LLMs，而专门针对医学的LLMs应用较少。评估方面，自动评估主要关注生成质量和任务性能，而人工评估则侧重于准确性、完整性、相关性和流畅性，但对偏见和安全的考量不足。RAG在医学领域的应用集中在问答、报告生成、文本摘要和信息提取等方面。

Conclusion: 医学RAG技术仍处于发展的早期阶段。为了实现可信赖和负责任的全球应用，未来的研究需要在临床验证、跨语言适应以及支持低资源环境方面取得显著进步。特别需要加强对模型偏见和安全性的评估，并探索利用医学专业LLMs和私有数据的潜力。

Abstract: The rapid growth of medical knowledge and increasing complexity of clinical practice pose challenges. In this context, large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated value; however, inherent limitations remain. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) technologies show potential to enhance their clinical applicability. This study reviewed RAG applications in medicine. We found that research primarily relied on publicly available data, with limited application in private data. For retrieval, approaches commonly relied on English-centric embedding models, while LLMs were mostly generic, with limited use of medical-specific LLMs. For evaluation, automated metrics evaluated generation quality and task performance, whereas human evaluation focused on accuracy, completeness, relevance, and fluency, with insufficient attention to bias and safety. RAG applications were concentrated on question answering, report generation, text summarization, and information extraction. Overall, medical RAG remains at an early stage, requiring advances in clinical validation, cross-linguistic adaptation, and support for low-resource settings to enable trustworthy and responsible global use.

### [78] [Behavior Modeling for Training-free Building of Private Domain Multi Agent System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10283)
*Won Ik Cho,Woonghee Han,Kyung Seo Ki,Young Min Kim*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种无需训练或数据生成的私域多agent对话系统框架，该框架通过行为建模和文档化来应对私域应用中的挑战，如工具异构性、领域特定术语、API可访问性受限和复杂治理等。通过简单地假设一个协调器、一个工具调用agent和一个通用聊天agent，并利用结构化规范和领域信息指令来定义工具集成，该框架实现了可扩展的私域工具适应性和上下文演变，而无需持续再训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）的出现使得具有编排、工具使用和对话能力的agent系统日益 visible。然而，将现有的开放域框架应用于私域面临诸多挑战，包括工具格式异构、领域特定术语、API可访问性受限以及复杂的治理问题。传统的解决方案（如在合成对话数据上进行微调）成本高昂、适应性差，并且可能损害通用性能。因此，研究如何有效地在私域中应用agent系统具有重要意义。

Method: 本研究提出的框架避免了训练和数据生成，采用了行为建模和文档化的方法。其设计包含一个协调器、一个工具调用agent和一个通用聊天agent。工具的集成通过结构化规范和领域信息指令来定义。这种方法支持工具的轻量级部署、利用API规范作为检索资源以及生成用于评估的合成对话。

Result: 该框架通过行为建模和文档化，成功实现了对私域工具和不断变化的上下文的可扩展适应，而无需持续的再训练。它为私域多agent对话系统的轻量级部署、利用API规范作为检索资源以及生成合成对话以供评估提供了支持，从而为在私域对话生态系统中对齐agent行为与领域专业知识提供了一种可持续的方法。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种创新的私域多agent对话系统框架，通过行为建模和文档化，解决了传统方法在私域应用中的痛点。该框架无需训练和数据生成，能够灵活适应私域环境和不断变化的上下文，为私域agent系统的开发和部署提供了可持续且高效的解决方案。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的agent交互模式和更广泛的领域应用。

Abstract: The rise of agentic systems that combine orchestration, tool use, and conversational capabilities, has been more visible by the recent advent of large language models (LLMs). While open-domain frameworks exist, applying them in private domains remains difficult due to heterogeneous tool formats, domain-specific jargon, restricted accessibility of APIs, and complex governance. Conventional solutions, such as fine-tuning on synthetic dialogue data, are burdensome and brittle under domain shifts, and risk degrading general performance. In this light, we introduce a framework for private-domain multi-agent conversational systems that avoids training and data generation by adopting behavior modeling and documentation. Our design simply assumes an orchestrator, a tool-calling agent, and a general chat agent, with tool integration defined through structured specifications and domain-informed instructions. This approach enables scalable adaptation to private tools and evolving contexts without continual retraining. The framework supports practical use cases, including lightweight deployment of multi-agent systems, leveraging API specifications as retrieval resources, and generating synthetic dialogue for evaluation -- providing a sustainable method for aligning agent behavior with domain expertise in private conversational ecosystems.

### [79] [The Data Fusion Labeler (dFL): Challenges and Solutions to Data Harmonization, Labeling, and Provenance in Fusion Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09725)
*Craig Michoski,Matthew Waller,Brian Sammuli,Zeyu Li,Tapan Ganatma Nakkina,Raffi Nazikian,Sterling Smith,David Orozco,Dongyang Kuang,Martin Foltin,Erik Olofsson,Mike Fredrickson,Jerry Louis-Jeune,David R. Hatch,Todd A. Oliver,Mitchell Clark,Steph-Yves Louis*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种名为数据融合标注器（dFL）的工具，用于处理和融合聚变能源研究中遇到的异构、多模态数据集。dFL通过不确定性感知的数据协调、模式兼容的数据融合以及可溯源的手动和自动标注，显著提高了数据分析效率（>50倍），增强了标注质量，并实现了跨设备的可比性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚变能源研究需要整合来自高分辨率诊断、控制系统和多尺度模拟的异构、多模态数据集。这些数据的数量巨大且复杂，因此需要新的工具来系统地协调和提取不同模式下的知识，以应对数据分析的挑战。

Method: dFL是一个统一的工作流程工具，它将对齐、归一化和标注嵌入到一个可重复的、操作顺序感知的框架中。该工具支持不确定性感知的数据协调、模式兼容的数据融合以及大规模的可追溯手动和自动标注。

Result: dFL将时间分析时间缩短了50倍以上，使得每小时能够持续标注超过200个样本，而不是每天只能标注几个。此外，它还提高了标签质量，从而提高了训练质量，并实现了跨设备的可比性。dFL在DIII-D的案例研究中成功应用于自动ELM检测和约束模式分类。

Conclusion: dFL作为一种核心工具，能够显著提高聚变能源数据分析的效率和质量，为数据驱动的发现、模型验证和未来燃烧等离子体装置的实时控制提供了潜力。尽管dFL在处理复杂数据集和提高分析效率方面表现出色，但未来的研究可以进一步探索其在更广泛数据集和实时控制场景下的应用。

Abstract: Fusion energy research increasingly depends on the ability to integrate heterogeneous, multimodal datasets from high-resolution diagnostics, control systems, and multiscale simulations. The sheer volume and complexity of these datasets demand the development of new tools capable of systematically harmonizing and extracting knowledge across diverse modalities. The Data Fusion Labeler (dFL) is introduced as a unified workflow instrument that performs uncertainty-aware data harmonization, schema-compliant data fusion, and provenance-rich manual and automated labeling at scale. By embedding alignment, normalization, and labeling within a reproducible, operator-order-aware framework, dFL reduces time-to-analysis by greater than 50X (e.g., enabling >200 shots/hour to be consistently labeled rather than a handful per day), enhances label (and subsequently training) quality, and enables cross-device comparability. Case studies from DIII-D demonstrate its application to automated ELM detection and confinement regime classification, illustrating its potential as a core component of data-driven discovery, model validation, and real-time control in future burning plasma devices.

</details>


### [80] [Plasma hydrodynamics from mean force kinetic theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09786)
*Jarett LeVan,Scott D. Baalrud*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用均力动理学理论计算了两组分（离子-电子）等离子体的电导率、热导率、电热系数、热电系数和剪切粘度，并将结果与分子动力学模拟进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统理论在库仑耦合强度大于100倍时会失效，但本文旨在通过均力动理学理论扩展流体力学到更广泛的等离子体密度范围。

Method: 使用均力动理学理论计算，并通过假设所有相互作用为排斥性库仑力，利用分子动力学模拟进行验证。

Result: 在库仑耦合强度高达约20时，所有系数均显示出与分子动力学模拟的良好一致性，远超传统理论的适用范围。

Conclusion: 均力动理学理论能够将流体力学理论扩展到高密度等离子体，并能准确预测其输运性质。

Abstract: Mean force kinetic theory is used to evaluate the electrical conductivity, thermal conductivity, electrothermal coefficient, thermoelectric coefficient, and shear viscosity of a two-component (ion-electron) plasma. Results are compared with molecular dynamics simulations. These simulations are made possible by assuming a repulsive Coulomb force for all interactions. Good agreement is found for all coefficients up to a Coulomb coupling strength of $Γ\approx 20$. This is over 100-times larger than the coupling strength at which traditional theories break down. It is concluded that mean force kinetic theory provides a means to extend hydrodynamics to dense plasmas.

</details>


### [81] [Tailored Three Dimensional Betatron Dynamics in UltraStable Hybrid Laser Plasma RF Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10096)
*A. A. Molavi Choobini,M. Shahmansouri*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本研究深入探讨了混合激光-等离子体射频加速器的理论和数值模拟，重点关注横向束流动力学、贝塔衰变极化和辐射反应。通过结合分析模型（时空等离子体尾场调制、依赖相位的射频驱动振荡、量子修正的Landau Lifshitz辐射反应）和全自洽三维粒子追踪模拟（EPOCH），研究人员证明了射频幅值、频率和相位能够精确控制横向聚焦强度、贝塔衰变振荡幅值和极化状态。结果显示，射频场与自然贝塔衰变频率的共振对齐可以放大横向位移，并通过增强的聚焦梯度和辐射反应抑制寄生振荡，从而减小发射率并减轻类似同步辐射的能量损失。稳定性图和三维力场揭示了对相位的高度敏感性，初始条件和射频分量比例决定了贝塔衰变幅值的时间演化，纵向场梯度则调节了γ增长率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在超相对论电子束中实现对横向动力学、极化和辐射反应的精确控制，本研究旨在探索混合激光-等离子体射频加速器的潜在能力。该研究解决了在现有加速器技术中难以同时实现高粒子束质量和高能量增益的挑战，并寻求一种能够有效调控电子束横向行为和辐射特性的新方法。

Method: 本研究采用理论分析与全自洽三维粒子追踪模拟相结合的方法。理论模型包括时空等离子体尾场调制、依赖相位的射频驱动振荡以及量子修正的Landau Lifshitz辐射反应。模拟工具为EPOCH代码。通过这些方法，研究人员对超相对论电子束在混合激光-等离子体射频加速器中的行为进行了详细研究。

Result: 研究结果表明，射频的幅值、频率和相位能够精确地控制横向聚焦强度、贝塔衰变振荡幅值和极化状态。当射频场与自然贝塔衰变频率发生共振对齐时，横向位移会得到放大，同时通过增强的聚焦梯度和辐射反应抑制寄生振荡，进而减小发射率并减轻能量损失。稳定性图和三维力场分析揭示了相位敏感性，即初始条件和射频分量比例会影响贝塔衰变幅值的时间演化，而纵向场梯度则能调制γ增长率。

Conclusion: 本研究为理解混合激光-等离子体射频系统中非线性、共振和阻尼现象提供了全面的认识。研究结果突显了在超相对论电子束中，对横向、纵向和极化动力学进行全谱调控的可能性，为未来高精度粒子加速器的设计和优化提供了重要的理论指导和实验依据。

Abstract: The detailed theoretical and numerical investigation of hybrid laser plasma RF accelerators, elucidating the mechanisms governing transverse beam dynamics, betatron polarization, and radiation reaction in ultra-relativistic electron bunches is presented. This framework combines analytical models of spatiotemporal plasma wakefield modulation, phase-dependent RF-driven oscillations, and quantum-corrected Landau Lifshitz radiation reaction with fully self-consistent 3D particle in cell simulations using EPOCH. The results demonstrate that RF amplitude, frequency, and phase enable precise control over transverse focusing strengths, betatron oscillation amplitudes, and polarization states. Resonant alignment between RF fields and natural betatron frequencies amplifies transverse excursions while damping parasitic oscillations through enhanced focusing gradients and radiation reaction, yielding reductions in emittance and mitigation of synchrotron-like energy losses. Stability maps and 3D force landscapes reveal strong phase sensitivity, where initial conditions and RF component ratios govern the temporal evolution of betatron amplitudes, and longitudinal field gradients modulate γ growth rates. These findings provide a comprehensive picture of nonlinear, resonant, and damping phenomena in hybrid laser plasma RF systems, highlighting the full spectrum of controllable transverse, longitudinal, and polarization dynamics in ultra relativistic electron beams.

</details>


### [82] [Molecular Dynamics Simulation of Hydrodynamic Transport Coefficients in Plasmas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09787)
*Briggs Damman,Jarett LeVan,Scott Baalrud*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 该研究使用分子动力学模拟计算了在广泛的库仑耦合强度范围内（0.01 ≤ Γ ≤ 140）两组分等离子体的输运系数。研究结果表明，在弱耦合区域（Γ ≲ 0.1），分子动力学模拟结果与 Chapman-Enskog 理论在仔细考虑线性本构关系定义的情况下表现出良好的一致性。然而，在强耦合区域（Γ ≫ 1），除了电阻率之外，其他输运系数的势能和维里分量会发散，只有动能分量才是有意义的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过第一性原理的分子动力学（MD）模拟，在广泛的库仑耦合强度下，检验 Chapman-Enskog 理论在弱耦合区域的标准结果，并探索强耦合区域输运系数的行为。这对于理解等离子体输运性质，特别是在不同耦合强度下的行为至关重要，也强调了在理论模型中正确处理线性本构关系定义的重要性。

Method: 研究采用了分子动力学（MD）模拟方法，并结合格林-久保（Green-Kubo）形式主义来计算两组分等离子体的输运系数。模拟在0.01 ≤ Γ ≤ 140的库仑耦合强度范围内进行。计算的输运系数包括热导率、电导率、热电系数和剪切粘度。研究中特别关注了在 Chapman-Enskog 理论框架下，不同输运系数的势能、维里和动能分量随耦合强度的变化。

Result: 在弱耦合区域（Γ ≲ 0.1），MD模拟结果与 Chapman-Enskog 理论结果吻合良好，前提是理论模型中对线性本构关系的定义得到仔细处理。研究表明，Chapman-Enskog 理论中的热导率是其热导率、热电系数和电导率的线性组合。在所研究的整个耦合强度范围内，可以获得有意义的电导率结果。然而，在强耦合区域（Γ ≫ 1），除了电导率（或其电阻率分量）外，其他输运系数的势能和维里分量均出现发散，只有动能分量保持有意义。

Conclusion: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟，为理解不同耦合强度下等离子体的输运性质提供了第一性原理的见解。研究证实了在弱耦合区域，理论与模拟结果的一致性，但强调了正确处理线性本构关系定义的重要性。同时，研究揭示了在强耦合区域，输运系数的有效性会受到限制，只有动能分量在经典等离子体中才是有意义的。未来的工作可以进一步探索强耦合区域的输运性质，以及考虑量子效应的影响。

Abstract: Molecular dynamics (MD) simulations are used to calculate transport coefficients in a two-component plasma interacting through a repulsive Coulomb potential. The thermal conductivity, electrical conductivity, electrothermal coefficient, thermoelectric coefficient, and shear viscosity are computed using the Green-Kubo formalism over a broad range of Coulomb coupling strength, $0.01 \leq Γ\leq 140$. Emphasis is placed on testing standard results of the Chapman-Enskog solution in the weakly coupled regime ($Γ\ll 1$) using these first-principles simulations. As expected, the results show good agreement for $Γ\lesssim 0.1$. However, this agreement is only possible if careful attention is paid to the definitions of linear constitutive relations in each of the theoretical models, a point that is often overlooked. For example, the standard Green-Kubo expression for thermal conductivity is a linear combination of thermal conductivity, electrothermal and thermoelectric coefficients computed in the Chapman-Enskog formalism. Meaningful results for electrical conductivity are obtained over the full range of coupling strengths explored, but it is shown that potential and virial components of the other transport coefficients diverge in the strongly coupled regime ($Γ\gg 1$). In this regime, only the kinetic components of the transport coefficients are meaningful for a classical plasma.

</details>


### [83] [$π$-PIC: a framework for modular particle-in-cell developments and simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09950)
*Frida Brogren,Christoffer Olofsson,Joel Magnusson,Arkady Gonoskov*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个Python控制的框架，用于整合、交叉测试和比较粒子 in Cell (PIC) 方法的各种求解器和扩展，旨在促进新技术在PIC模拟中的应用。该框架支持Python以及C++和Fortran等低级语言编写的求解器，并展示了其在处理QED过程、移动窗口和激光脉冲聚焦等高级功能方面的灵活性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的PIC方法存在一些长期存在的问题，例如物理守恒量的精确保持和无偏的集合降采样。这些限制阻碍了PIC代码在更低分辨率和更少粒子数下运行的能力。为了克服这些限制，需要新的PIC方法，并需要一个易于使用的框架来促进这些新方法的传播和应用，从而实现更高效的PIC模拟。

Method: 本文提出并实现了一个Python控制的框架，该框架提供了统一的接口，能够整合、交叉测试和比较不同的PIC求解器及扩展。该框架支持用Python或C++、Fortran等低级语言编写的求解器。为了验证框架的灵活性，研究人员实现了并测试了多种PIC求解器，以及能够管理量子电动力学（QED）过程、移动窗口和激光脉冲紧聚焦功能的扩展。

Result: 框架成功地集成了多种PIC求解器和扩展，并展示了其处理QED过程、移动窗口和激光脉冲紧聚焦等复杂功能的灵活性。通过统一的接口，该框架能够方便地对不同的PIC求解器和算法进行交叉测试和比较，为评估和推广新的PIC技术提供了有效的平台。

Conclusion: 所提出的Python控制框架能够有效地促进新一代PIC方法的发展和应用，通过提供统一的接口来整合、测试和比较各种PIC求解器和扩展。这有助于克服传统PIC方法的局限性，推动PIC模拟技术在个人计算机和超级计算机上的广泛应用，并加速科学发现。

Abstract: Recently proposed modifications of the standard particle-in-cell (PIC) method resolve long-standing limitations such as exact preservation of physically conserved quantities and unbiased ensemble down-sampling. Such advances pave the way for next-generation PIC codes capable of using lower resolution and fewer particles per cell, enabling interactive studies on personal computers and facilitating large-scale parameter scans on supercomputers. Here, we present a Python-controlled framework designed to stimulate the dissemination and adoption of novel PIC developments by providing unified interfaces for accommodation, cross-testing, and comparison of PIC solvers and extensions written in Python or low-level languages like C++ and Fortran. To demonstrate flexibility of proposed interfaces we present and test implementations of several PIC solvers, as well as of extensions that is capable of managing QED processes, moving-window, and tight focusing of laser pulses.

</details>


### [84] [Microscopy X-ray Imaging enriched with Small Angle X-ray Scattering for few nanometer resolution reveals shock waves and compression in intense short pulse laser irradiation of solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10127)
*Thomas Kluge,Arthur Hirsch-Passicos,Jannis Schulz,Mungo Frost,Eric Galtier,Maxence Gauthier,Jörg Grenzer,Christian Gutt,Lingen Huang,Uwe Hübner,Megan Ikeya,Hae Ja Lee,Dimitri Khaghani,Willow Moon Martin,Brian Edward Marré,Motoaki Nakatsutsumi,Paweł Ordyna,Franziska-Luise Paschke-Brühl,Alexander Pelka,Lisa Randolph,Hans-Peter Schlenvoigt,Christopher Schoenwaelder,Michal Šmíd,Long Yang,Ulrich Schramm,Thomas E. Cowan*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出并验证了一种结合X射线成像（XRM）和X射线小角散射（SAXS）的诊断方法，首次实现了对激光驱动的高能量密度状态下冲击波的形成和衰减进行纳尺度精度的直接观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解激光脉冲如何将固体压缩成高能量密度状态，需要能够同时解析宏观几何结构和纳米尺度结构的诊断技术。现有的诊断方法在跨越宏观和微观尺度方面存在不足，阻碍了对激光驱动的冲击波动力学过程的深入理解，这对于惯性约束聚变、温密物质物理以及行星物理等研究至关重要。

Method: 研究人员在LCLS的极端条件物质（MEC）终端，使用45飞秒、0.9焦耳、800纳米的激光脉冲（强度为3.5e19 W/cm2）辐照25微米厚的铜线，并利用8.2 keV的X射线自由电子激光（XFEL）脉冲进行探测。他们结合了X射线成像（XRM）技术来可视化烧蚀、压缩和向内传播的前沿演化，分辨率约为200纳米；同时利用X射线小角散射（SAXS）技术，通过时间分辨的散射条纹演化来量化这些前沿的纳米尺度锐度。

Result: XRM技术清晰地展示了烧蚀、压缩以及向内传播的前沿演化过程，分辨率达到约200纳米。SAXS技术则通过时间分辨的散射条纹演化，量化了这些前沿的纳米尺度锐度。联合分析揭示，最初光滑的压缩在约18皮秒后会锐化成纳米尺度的冲击波前沿，这与分析陡化模型和流体动力学模拟结果一致。该冲击波前沿速度约为25公里/秒，横向宽度达数十微米。研究首次实现了对固体密度下冲击波形成和衰减的直接观测，精度达到纳米尺度。

Conclusion: 这项集成的XRM-SAXS方法成功地弥合了宏观几何和纳米结构之间的诊断差距，为研究激光驱动的冲击波提供了定量、多尺度的诊断手段。该方法对于理解惯性约束聚变、温密物质以及行星物理等领域中的高能量密度物理过程具有重要意义。未来的工作可以进一步探索该方法在不同材料和不同极端条件下的应用，以期更全面地理解物质在极端状态下的行为。

Abstract: Understanding how laser pulses compress solids into high-energy-density states requires diagnostics that simultaneously resolve macroscopic geometry and nanometer-scale structure. Here we present a combined X-ray imaging (XRM) and small-angle X-ray scattering (SAXS) approach that bridges this diagnostic gap. Using the Matter in Extreme Conditions end station at LCLS, we irradiated 25-micrometer copper wires with 45-fs, 0.9-J, 800-nm pulses at 3.5e19 W/cm2 while probing with 8.2-keV XFEL pulses. XRM visualizes the evolution of ablation, compression, and inward-propagating fronts with about 200-nm resolution, while SAXS quantifies their nanometer-scale sharpness through the time-resolved evolution of scattering streaks. The joint analysis reveals that an initially smooth compression steepens into a nanometer-sharp shock front after roughly 18 ps, consistent with an analytical steepening model and hydrodynamic simulations. The front reaches a velocity of about 25 km/s and a lateral width of several tens of micrometers, demonstrating for the first time the direct observation of shock formation and decay at solid density with few-nanometer precision. This integrated XRM-SAXS method establishes a quantitative, multiscale diagnostic of laser-driven shocks in dense plasmas relevant to inertial confinement fusion, warm dense matter, and planetary physics.

</details>


### [85] [Self-organisation through layering of $β$-plane like turbulence in plasmas and geophysical fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10438)
*P. L. Guillon,G. Dif-Pradalier,Y. Sarazin,D. W. Hughes,Ö. D. Gürcan*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在保守势涡模型中，等离子体和地球物理流体中阶梯状形成和分层的机制。研究了湍流自组织和非线性饱和，对比了不同自由能产生机制（强迫或线性不稳定性）以及标准或修正的纬向流响应。结果表明，标准纬向响应的β平面湍流会形成逐渐合并的大尺度椭圆纬向结构，无论驱动方式如何。而具有修正纬向响应的等离子体系统能快速形成大小明确的直线、静止喷流，同样与驱动方式无关。此外，等离子体系统表现出从纬向流主导态到涡旋主导态的相变，且饱和无需大尺度摩擦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在理解和对比在等离子体和地球物理流体中观察到的阶梯状形成和分层现象。这些现象在理解湍流自组织、非线性饱和以及能量耗散机制方面具有重要意义，对于解释天体物理现象（如行星大气环流）和约束聚变等离子体至关重要。通过研究不同驱动机制和纬向流响应下的差异，可以揭示产生这些结构的基本物理原理。

Method: 该研究采用了简化的、势涡守恒的模型来研究阶梯状形成和分层。具体方法包括：1. 模拟标准和修正的Charney-Hasegawa-Mima（CHM）方程，并施加随机强迫。2. 建立并研究两种简单的由不稳定性驱动的模型：一种源于等离子体，另一种源于地球物理背景。3. 对比这两种不同驱动方式（强迫和不稳定性）以及两种不同纬向流响应（标准和修正）下的模拟结果。

Result: 研究观察到，在标准纬向响应下（不区分纬向和非纬向扰动），β平面湍流（无论由慢速强迫还是斜压不稳定性驱动）会逐渐形成大尺度、椭圆形的纬向结构，并逐渐合并。相反，修正了纬向响应的等离子体系统（无论由随机强迫还是耗散漂移不稳定性驱动）能快速形成大小明确、静止的直线型喷流。此外，等离子体系统在纬向流主导态和涡旋主导态之间表现出相变现象，且在两种状态下均能实现无需大尺度摩擦的饱和。

Conclusion: 该研究通过比较不同驱动机制和纬向流响应下的势涡守恒模型，揭示了等离子体和地球物理流体中阶梯状形成和分层的不同动力学过程。标准纬向响应倾向于形成合并的椭圆结构，而修正的纬向响应则能快速形成直线喷流。等离子体系统中的相变现象和无需大尺度摩擦的饱和机制为理解复杂流体系统提供新见解。未来的工作可以进一步探索这些模型在更复杂场景下的适用性，并尝试进行实验验证。

Abstract: Staircase formation and layering is studied in simplified, potential vorticity conserving models of plasmas and geophysical fluids, by investigating turbulent self-organisation and nonlinear saturation with different mechanisms of free energy production -- forcing or linear instability -- and with standard or modified zonal flow responses. To this end, staircase formation in both the standard and modified Charney-Hasegawa-Mima equations with stochastic forcing, along with two different simple instability driven models -- one from a plasma and from a geophysical context -- are studied and compared. In these studies, it is observed that $β$-plane turbulence that does not distinguish between zonal and non-zonal perturbations (i.e., standard zonal response) gradually forms large-scale, elliptic zonal structures that merge progressively, regardless of whether it is driven by forcing (though it should be slow enough to allow wave couplings) or by the baroclinic instability, using for example a two-layer model. Conversely, the plasma system, with its modified zonal response, can rapidly form straight, stationary jets of well-defined size, again regardless of the way it is driven: by stochastic forcing or by the dissipative drift instability. Furthermore, the instability-driven plasma system exhibits a phase transition between a zonal flow dominated state and an eddy dominated state. In both states, saturation is possible without large-scale friction.

</details>


### [86] [Axisymmetric Gyrokinetic Simulation of ASDEX-Upgrade Scrape-off Layer Using a Conservative Implicit BGK Collision Operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22821)
*D. Liu,J. Juno,G. W. Hammett,A. Hakim,A. Shukla,M. Francisquez*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文实现并验证了一种隐式碰撞算子，显著提高了高碰撞性聚变等离子体模拟的计算效率，同时保持了准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高碰撞性聚变等离子体模拟中，显式时间积分方案在解决碰撞物理时面临时间步长限制，导致计算成本过高。

Method: 在Gkeyll框架的DG全f回旋动力学求解器中，实现了一个隐式BGK碰撞算子。该算子结合了无碰撞平流的显式时间积分器，并采用迭代方案修正离散近似到平衡麦克斯韦分布，以保证守恒性。该方法被推广以处理跨物种碰撞，并与LBD算子进行基准测试。

Result: 与LBD算子相比，隐式BGK算子使ASDEX-Upgrade剥离层二维轴对称模拟速度提高了56倍，且在较低分辨率下即可收敛。在高碰撞性极限下，隐式BGK算子的模拟结果与LBD算子高度一致。

Conclusion: 本文提出的隐式、守恒且支持跨物种碰撞的BGK算子，有效解决了高碰撞性聚变等离子体模拟的计算效率瓶颈，并在与LBD算子的对比中验证了其准确性。未来可进一步探索其在更广泛模拟场景中的应用。

Abstract: Collisions play an important role in turbulence and transport of fusion plasmas. For kinetic simulations, as the collisionality increases in the domain of interest, the size of the time step to resolve the collisional physics can become overly restrictive in an explicit time integration scheme, leading to high computational cost. With the aim of overcoming such restriction, we have implemented an implicit Bhatnagar-Gross-Krook (BGK) collision operator for use in the discontinuous Galerkin (DG) full-f gyrokinetic solver within the Gkeyll framework, which, when combined with Gkeyll's traditional explicit time integrator for collisionless advection, can significantly increase the time step in gyrokinetic simulations of highly collisional regimes. To ensure conservation of density, momentum, and energy, we utilize an iterative scheme to correct the discretized approximation to the equilibrium Maxwellian distribution to which the BGK collision operator relaxes. We have further generalized the BGK infrastructure, both the implicit scheme and the correction routine, to handle cross species collisions. This improved implicit and conservative BGK operator is benchmarked against the more accurate but more computationally expensive Lenard-Bernstein-Dougherty (LBD) operator which has been utilized in prior studies with Gkeyll. The implicit BGK operator enables 2D axisymmetric simulations of the ASDEX-Upgrade scrape-off layer to run 56 times faster to completion than the simulations with the LBD operator, because the BGK operator is more robust and converges at a lower resolution than is required by the LBD operator. Additionally, in this more collisional limit, we demonstrate that the results of our simulations utilizing the implicit BGK operator agreed well with simulations utilizing the more computationally expensive LBD operator.

</details>

### [87] [Localized kernel gradient correction for SPH simulations of water wave propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10064)
*Lennart Justin Schulze,Vito Zago,Giuseppe Bilotta,Robert Anthony Dalrymple*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: SPH模型在模拟水波传播时存在数值耗散问题，本文提出了一种基于水波力学判据的局部高阶格式，仅在部分区域使用高阶格式，从而在保证精度的前提下减少计算量，并解决了自由表面处的核梯度校正问题，在站立波和行波模拟中均取得满意结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础SPH模型在模拟水波传播时存在过度的数值耗散，影响模拟精度。现有的高阶方法（如核梯度校正）虽然能提高精度，但会增加计算成本。因此，需要一种在保证精度的同时优化计算效率的方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于水波力学判据的局部高阶SPH方法。该方法根据水波力学的特征，区分需要特殊处理的粒子和不需要的粒子，仅对部分粒子采用高阶格式。此外，还提出了一种解决自由表面核梯度校正问题的方案。

Result: 该方法在模拟一个盆地中的驻波和一个长波水槽中的行波时，均取得了满意的结果。与传统方法相比，该方法在保证精度的前提下，有望节省大量的计算资源，尤其是在深水波模拟中。

Conclusion: 本文提出的局部高阶SPH方法，能够有效解决水波传播模拟中的数值耗散问题，并在计算效率和模拟精度之间取得了良好的平衡。该方法尤其适用于深水波的模拟，具有潜在的应用价值。未来的工作可以进一步探索该方法的适用范围和优化其算法以适应更复杂的水波现象。

Abstract: Basic Smoothed Particle Hydrodynamics (SPH) models exhibit excessive, numerical dissipation in the simulation of water wave propagation. This can be remedied using higher-order approaches such as kernel gradient correction, which introduce additional computational effort. The present work demonstrates, that the higher-order scheme is only required in a limited part of the water wave in order to obtain satisfying results. The criterion for distinguishing particles in need of special treatment from those that do not is motivated by water wave mechanics. Especially for deep water waves, the approach potentially spares large amounts of computational effort. The present paper also proposes a remedy for issues of the kernel gradient correction occurring at the free surface. Satisfying results for the proposed approach are shown for a standing wave in a basin and a progressive wave train in a long wave tank.

### [88] [Phase field modelling of cracking and capacity fade in core-shell cathode particles for lithium-ion batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10355)
*Y. Tu,B. Wu,E. Martínez-Pañeda*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种计算框架，用于预测和理解锂离子电池中核壳结构电极的机械失效及其对电池性能的影响。研究发现，表面裂缝的产生与锂浓度在核壳间的差异有关，而界面脱粘则源于应力集中，这两种失效模式都会导致容量损失。该框架可用于优化电极材料设计，延长电池寿命。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锂离子电池的高性能化对高性能电极材料提出了更高的要求。核壳结构电极被认为是提高能量密度和功率密度的有前景的策略。然而，实验观察表明，核壳结构在充放电过程中容易发生机械失效，如壳层开裂和核壳界面脱粘，导致电池性能下降。理解这些失效机制及其对电池性能的影响，对于设计更稳定、寿命更长的核壳结构电极至关重要。

Method: 本研究开发了一个全面的计算框架，该框架能够模拟核壳结构电极在充放电过程中的化学-力学-损伤耦合行为。利用相场法来捕捉宏观材料断裂和界面脱粘。该模型能够量化颗粒开裂和容量衰减。通过对代表性的核壳体系（NMC811@NMC532）进行案例研究，以量化颗粒开裂的严重程度和容量损失。

Result: 研究结果表明，当核部锂浓度显著高于壳部时，会出现表面裂缝。由于壳层膨胀更大，界面附近的局部环向应力导致界面脱粘。界面脱粘会迅速发展，阻碍锂离子传输，可能导致单次放电后容量损失超过10%。对于较大的颗粒，裂纹扩展可能导致整个颗粒破碎。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的计算框架能够深入揭示核壳结构电极的失效机制，并为设计具有更高性能和更长寿命的电极材料提供指导。通过模拟核壳体系的失效行为，为优化电池材料的设计提供了有价值的见解。

Abstract: Core-shell electrode particles are a promising morphology control strategy for high-performance lithium-ion batteries. However, experimental observations reveal that these structures remain prone to mechanical failure, with shell fractures and core-shell debonding occurring after a single charge. In this work, we present a novel, comprehensive computational framework to predict and gain insight into the failure of core-shell morphologies and the associated degradation in battery performance. The fully coupled chemo-mechano-damage model presented captures the interplay between mechanical damage and electrochemical behaviours, enabling the quantification of particle cracking and capacity fade. Both bulk material fracture and interface debonding are captured by utilising the phase field method. We quantify the severity of particle cracking and capacity loss through case studies on a representative core-shell system (NMC811@NMC532). The results bring valuable insights into cracking patterns, underlying mechanisms, and their impact on capacity loss. Surface cracks are found to initiate when a significantly higher lithium concentration accumulates in the core compared to the shell. Interfacial debonding is shown to arise from localised hoop stresses near the core-shell interface, due to greater shell expansion. This debonding develops rapidly, impedes lithium-ion transport, and can lead to more than 10\% capacity loss after a single discharge. Furthermore, larger particles may experience crack branching driven by extensive tensile zones, potentially fragmenting the entire particle. The framework developed can not only bring new insight into the degradation mechanisms of core-shell particles but also be used to design electrode materials with improved performance and extended lifetime.

</details>


### [89] [Robust AI-ECG for Predicting Left Ventricular Systolic Dysfunction in Pediatric Congenital Heart Disease](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.19564)
*Yuting Yang,Lorenzo Peracchio,Joshua Mayourian,John K. Triedman,Timothy Miller,William G. La Cava*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在数据资源有限的情况下训练人工智能心电图（AI-ECG）模型以检测儿童先天性心脏病左心室收缩功能障碍的方法。通过引入“在流形上的对抗性扰动”策略生成合成噪声样本，并结合“不确定性感知对抗性训练”算法，在真实数据集上验证了该方法的有效性，实现了低成本、可靠的检测，特别适用于资源受限的临床环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种新的训练框架，包括两个关键部分：1. “在流形上的对抗性扰动”策略，用于生成更能反映真实信号变化的合成噪声样本，以扩充有限的数据集。2. “不确定性感知对抗性训练”算法，该算法不依赖于特定模型架构，能够提高模型的鲁棒性。

Result: 在真实的儿科数据集上进行的评估表明，该方法能够以低成本和高可靠性检测左心室收缩功能障碍。具体性能指标和与现有方法的比较未在摘要中详细说明，但强调了其在资源受限环境中的潜力。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发了一种在数据有限的情况下训练AI-ECG模型的方法，解决了AI在基层医疗机构部署的瓶颈。该方法通过生成更真实的合成数据和提高模型鲁棒性，实现了可靠的左心室收缩功能障碍检测，为资源受限的临床环境提供了有价值的解决方案。未来的工作可能会进一步探索该方法的扩展性和在更多临床场景中的应用。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence-enhanced electrocardiogram (AI-ECG) has shown promise as an inexpensive, ubiquitous, and non-invasive screening tool to detect left ventricular systolic dysfunction in pediatric congenital heart disease. However, current approaches rely heavily on large-scale labeled datasets, which poses a major obstacle to the democratization of AI in hospitals where only limited pediatric ECG data are available. In this work, we propose a robust training framework to improve AI-ECG performance under low-resource conditions. Specifically, we introduce an on-manifold adversarial perturbation strategy for pediatric ECGs to generate synthetic noise samples that better reflect real-world signal variations. Building on this, we develop an uncertainty-aware adversarial training algorithm that is architecture-agnostic and enhances model robustness. Evaluation on the real-world pediatric dataset demonstrates that our method enables low-cost and reliable detection of left ventricular systolic dysfunction, highlighting its potential for deployment in resource-limited clinical settings.

### [90] [Boosting In-Silicon Directed Evolution with Fine-Tuned Protein Language Model and Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09900)
*Yaodong Yang,Yang Wang,Jinpeng Li,Pei Guo,Da Han,Guangyong Chen,Pheng-Ann Heng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为AlphaDE的新框架，该框架利用大型语言模型来指导蛋白质序列的进化搜索，以克服现有算法的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于硅的定向进化算法主要关注搜索策略，而忽略了利用编码丰富进化模式的蛋白质语言模型来指导搜索。本研究旨在弥合这一差距，通过利用大型语言模型的创新范式来进化蛋白质序列。

Method: AlphaDE框架首先通过在同源蛋白质序列上使用掩码语言建模来微调预训练的蛋白质语言模型，以激活目标蛋白质类别的进化合理性。然后，AlphaDE引入了基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的测试时推理，该推理能够有效地从微调后的蛋白质语言模型中获得进化指导来进化蛋白质。

Result: 实验结果表明，AlphaDE即使在进行少量微调的情况下，其性能也显著优于以前最先进的方法。此外，一个案例研究表明，AlphaDE可以通过计算进化来压缩蛋白质序列空间。

Conclusion: AlphaDE框架通过整合大型语言模型来指导蛋白质进化搜索，展示了显著的优势，并在性能和效率方面超越了现有方法。未来的工作可以探索将该框架应用于更广泛的蛋白质工程任务，并进一步优化模型以提高计算效率。

Abstract: Protein evolution through amino acid sequence mutations is a cornerstone of life sciences. While current in-silicon directed evolution algorithms focus on designing search strategies, they overlook how to utilize the transformative protein language models, which encode rich evolutionary patterns, to guide search. To bridge this gap, we propose AlphaDE, a novel framework to evolve protein sequences by harnessing the innovative paradigms of large language models. First, AlphaDE fine-tunes pretrained protein language models using masked language modeling on homologous protein sequences to activate the evolutionary plausibility for the interested protein class. Second, AlphaDE introduces test-time inference based on Monte Carlo tree search, which effectively evolves proteins with evolutionary guidance from the fine-tuned protein language model. Extensive benchmark experiments show that AlphaDE remarkably outperforms previous state-of-the-art methods even with few-shot fine-tuning. An interesting case study further shows that AlphaDE supports condensing the protein sequence space through computational evolution.

### [91] [An Efficient and Almost Optimal Solver for the Joint Routing-Assignment Problem via Partial JRA and Large-α Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09563)
*Qilong Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个名为部分路径重建（PPR）的新型求解器，用于解决联合路径分配（JRA）优化问题，该问题旨在同时确定物品到占位符的分配以及访问每个节点对一次的汉密尔顿循环，以最小化总旅行成本。与以往保证最优但计算效率低下的精确方法和近似率约为1%的启发式方法不同，PPR通过识别关键物品-占位符对形成一个简化的子问题来高效地优化全局解决方案。该框架结合了大型-α约束，并在基准数据集上进行了测试，结果显示对于大规模（n=300, 500, 1000）JRA问题，该方法能够以0.00%的平均偏差获得近乎最优的解决方案，同时保持高计算效率。此外，该方法还展示了在旅行商问题（TSP）及相关优化问题上的广泛应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联合路径分配（JRA）优化问题是一个复杂的组合优化问题，它要求同时解决物品到占位符的分配以及寻找一条访问所有节点对一次的汉密尔顿循环，目标是最小化总旅行成本。尽管已有精确的混合整数规划（MIP）求解器，但其计算复杂度限制了其在大规模问题上的应用。现有的启发式方法虽然提高了效率，但最优性偏差仍约为1%。因此，存在着对更高效、更高精度求解大规模JRA问题的迫切需求，以克服现有方法的局限性。

Method: 本研究提出了一种名为部分路径重建（PPR）的新型求解器来解决JRA问题。该方法首先识别关键的物品-占位符对，以构建一个简化的子问题，然后通过高效求解该子问题来优化全局解决方案。该方法被整合到一个名为PJAR的框架中，可以进一步改进初始的启发式合并解决方案，将偏差减半。此外，通过在优化路径上迭代地使用PPR求解器进行优化，可以获得高精度的路径。研究中还引入了一个全局大型-α约束来增强JRA模型的优化性。实验在包含n=300、500和1000个节点的大规模基准数据集上进行，以评估该方法的性能。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提出的PPR方法在处理大规模JRA问题（n=300, 500, 1000）时表现出色。与现有方法相比，该方法能够持续获得近乎最优的解决方案，平均偏差仅为0.00%，显著优于先前启发式方法约1%的偏差。同时，该方法在计算效率方面也表现出高度的竞争力，能够高效地处理大规模实例。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发了一种名为PPR的新型高效求解器，并将其应用于JRA优化问题。该方法通过识别关键对并构建简化子问题，实现了对大规模JRA问题的高精度（0.00%平均偏差）和高计算效率的求解。这克服了现有精确方法计算效率低下和启发式方法精度不足的缺点。此外，该研究提出的框架和方法论具有广泛的应用潜力，可推广至TSP及相关优化领域。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在其他复杂优化问题上的应用。

Abstract: The Joint Routing-Assignment (JRA) optimization problem simultaneously determines the assignment of items to placeholders and a Hamiltonian cycle that visits each node pair exactly once, with the objective of minimizing total travel cost. Previous studies introduced an exact mixed-integer programming (MIP) solver, along with datasets and a Gurobi implementation, showing that while the exact approach guarantees optimality, it becomes computationally inefficient for large-scale instances. To overcome this limitation, heuristic methods based on merging algorithms and shaking procedures were proposed, achieving solutions within approximately 1% deviation from the optimum. This work presents a novel and more efficient approach that attains high-accuracy, near-optimal solutions for large-scale JRA problems. The proposed method introduces a Partial Path Reconstructon (PPR) solver that first identifies key item-placeholder pairs to form a reduced subproblem, which is solved efficiently to refine the global solution. Using this PJAR framework, the initial heuristic merging solutions can be further improved, reducing the deviation by half. Moreover, the solution can be iteratively polished with PPR based solver along the optimization path to yield highly accurate tours. Additionally, a global Large-α constraint is incorporated into the JRA model to further enhance solution optimality. Experimental evaluations on benchmark datasets with n = 300, 500, and 1000 demonstrate that the proposed method consistently delivers almost optimal solutions, achieving an average deviation of 0.00% from the ground truth while maintaining high computational efficiency. Beyond the JRA problem, the proposed framework and methodologies exhibit strong potential for broader applications. The Framework can be applied to TSP and related optimization problems.

*David Woller,Viktor Kozák,Miroslav Kulich,Libor Přeučil*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出的方法基于可变邻域搜索（VNS）元启发式算法。VNS是一种用于求解组合优化问题的有效算法，它通过系统地搜索解的邻域来逐步改进解的质量。具体到CGVRP问题，VNS算法通过定义一系列邻域搜索算子，并在搜索过程中灵活切换这些算子，以跳出局部最优，寻找全局最优解。该方法在2020年IEEE世界计算智能大会的CEC-12竞赛中被用作参赛算法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于VNS的CGVRP方法在竞赛中取得了成功，并优于后续研究。这表明VNS元启发式算法在处理EVRP及其变体问题上具有巨大潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索VNS与其他优化技术的结合，以及在更复杂的EVRP变体上的应用，例如考虑充电站的动态调度、多类型车辆的混合使用等，以期为现实物流优化提供更全面的解决方案。

Abstract: The Electric Vehicle Routing Problem (EVRP) extends the classical Vehicle Routing Problem (VRP) to reflect the growing use of electric and hybrid vehicles in logistics. Due to the variety of constraints considered in the literature, comparing approaches across different problem variants remains challenging. A minimalistic variant of the EVRP, known as the Capacitated Green Vehicle Routing Problem (CGVRP), was the focus of the CEC-12 competition held during the 2020 IEEE World Congress on Computational Intelligence. This paper presents the competition-winning approach, based on the Variable Neighborhood Search (VNS) metaheuristic. The method achieves the best results on the full competition dataset and also outperforms a more recent algorithm published afterward.

### [95] [Rebellion: Noise-Robust Reasoning Training for Audio Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09682)
*Tiansheng Huang,Virat Shejwalkar,Oscar Chang,Milad Nasr,Ling Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究首次研究了音频推理模型（ARMs）在面对越狱攻击时的安全性。研究发现，标准的推理训练（RT）无法防御针对ARMs的“越狱”攻击，原因是“越狱”攻击会导致模型表示的显著漂移。为此，研究提出了名为Rebellion的新型鲁棒推理训练方法，旨在提高ARMs应对最坏情况表示漂移的能力。实验结果表明，Rebellion在不损害模型常规任务性能的前提下，能有效防御高级音频“越狱”攻击，并显著优化了准确性-安全性权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LMs）在推理能力上的提升，能够进行音频推理的音频大型模型（ARMs）日益受到关注。然而，目前尚未有研究关注ARMs在面对旨在诱导有害响应的“越狱”攻击时的安全性问题。因此，研究ARMs的安全性至关重要，尤其是在对抗日益复杂的“越狱”技术方面。

Method: 研究人员首先评估了标准推理训练（RT）方法在音频推理模型（ARMs）上的安全性，特别是针对“越狱”攻击。在发现标准RT无法防御由表示漂移引起的高级“越狱”攻击后，研究人员提出了一种名为Rebellion的新型鲁棒推理训练方法。Rebellion旨在训练ARMs在面对最坏情况下的表示漂移时仍能保持鲁棒性。所有实验均在Qwen2-Audio模型上进行。

Result: 实验结果显示，标准RT虽然能防御基础的音频“越狱”攻击，但对于研究人员提出的更复杂的“越狱”方法则无效，原因是这些攻击会导致目标ARMs产生显著的表示漂移。而提出的Rebellion方法，在Qwen2-Audio模型上进行了验证，证明了其不仅能防御高级音频“越狱”攻击，而且在不牺牲模型在正常任务上的性能的情况下，显著改善了准确性-安全性之间的权衡，优于标准的RT方法。

Conclusion: 本研究填补了音频推理模型（ARMs）安全性研究的空白，揭示了标准推理训练（RT）在防御“越狱”攻击方面的局限性。提出的Rebellion方法通过训练ARMs应对表示漂移，有效提升了模型的安全性，同时保持了其在常规任务上的性能。该研究为开发更安全、更可靠的ARMs提供了新的途径，并强调了在模型训练中考虑鲁棒性和安全性对抗的重要性。未来的工作可以进一步探索Rebellion的泛化能力以及在更多模型和攻击场景下的有效性。

Abstract: Instilling reasoning capabilities in large models (LMs) using reasoning training (RT) significantly improves LMs' performances. Thus Audio Reasoning Models (ARMs), i.e., audio LMs that can reason, are becoming increasingly popular. However, no work has studied the safety of ARMs against jailbreak attacks that aim to elicit harmful responses from target models. To this end, first, we show that standard RT with appropriate safety reasoning data can protect ARMs from vanilla audio jailbreaks, but cannot protect them against our proposed simple yet effective jailbreaks. We show that this is because of the significant representation drift between vanilla and advanced jailbreaks which forces the target ARMs to emit harmful responses. Based on this observation, we propose Rebellion, a robust RT that trains ARMs to be robust to the worst-case representation drift. All our results are on Qwen2-Audio; they demonstrate that Rebellion: 1) can protect against advanced audio jailbreaks without compromising performance on benign tasks, and 2) significantly improves accuracy-safety trade-off over standard RT method.

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used to annotate learning interactions, yet concerns about reliability limit their utility. Using transcripts from 30 one-to-one math sessions, we compare three production LLMs (GPT, Claude, Gemini) under three conditions: unverified annotation, self-verification, and cross-verification across all orchestration configurations. Outputs are benchmarked against a blinded, disagreement-focused human adjudication using Cohen's kappa. Overall, orchestration yields a 58 percent improvement in kappa. Self-verification nearly doubles agreement relative to unverified baselines, with the largest gains for challenging tutor moves. Cross-verification achieves a 37 percent improvement on average, with pair- and construct-dependent effects: some verifier-annotator pairs exceed self-verification, while others reduce alignment, reflecting differences in verifier strictness. We contribute: (1) a flexible orchestration framework instantiating control, self-, and cross-verification; (2) an empirical comparison across frontier LLMs on authentic tutoring data with blinded human "gold" labels; and (3) a concise notation, verifier(annotator) (e.g., Gemini(GPT) or Claude(Claude)), to standardize reporting and make directional effects explicit for replication. Results position verification as a principled design lever for reliable, scalable LLM-assisted annotation in Learning Analytics.

*Mar Canet Sola,Varvara Guljajeva*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前占主导地位的大型、闭源企业AI系统在互动艺术创作中带来了严峻挑战，包括内容过滤限制、保存问题、延迟增加和接口有限。这些问题严重限制了艺术家的创作自由和作品的长期可行性。因此，有必要探索一种能够赋予艺术家更多自主权、控制权和可持续性的替代方案。

Method: 本文采用论证和比较的方法。通过分析当前闭源大型AI系统在互动艺术中的局限性，论证了开放小型AI模型的优势。文章探讨了艺术家如何通过本地部署、控制基础设施和代码、自定义模型（通过代码修改或重新训练/微调）来利用小型AI模型，从而实现技术上的自决。

Result: 开放小型AI模型为互动艺术实践带来了创作自主权、控制权和可持续性。艺术家能够更长时间地使用模型，创建定制模型，并更好地控制作品的长期保存和展览。这与依赖不适合互动艺术需求的闭源企业AI形成了对比。

Conclusion: 开放小型AI模型为互动艺术领域提供了技术自决的途径，使艺术家能够更好地掌控其创作过程，并确保作品的长期保存和可持续性。虽然本文主要集中在理论和概念层面，但它为未来在互动艺术中应用和开发开放AI模型奠定了基础。未来的工作可以探索更具体的模型实现和集成策略，以及对艺术家工作流程的实际影响进行案例研究。

Abstract: This position paper argues for the importance of open small AI models in creative independence for interactive art practices. Deployable locally, these models offer artists vital control over infrastructure and code, unlike dominant large, closed-source corporate systems. Such centralized platforms function as opaque black boxes, imposing severe limitations on interactive artworks, including restrictive content filters, preservation issues, and technical challenges such as increased latency and limited interfaces. In contrast, small AI models empower creators with more autonomy, control, and sustainability for these artistic processes. They enable the ability to use a model as long as they want, create their own custom model, either by making code changes to integrate new interfaces, or via new datasets by re-training or fine-tuning the model. This fosters technological self-determination, offering greater ownership and reducing reliance on corporate AI ill-suited for interactive art's demands. Critically, this approach empowers the artist and supports long-term preservation and exhibition of artworks with AI components. This paper explores the practical applications and implications of using open small AI models in interactive art, contrasting them with closed-source alternatives.

### [98] [SlideBot: A Multi-Agent Framework for Generating Informative, Reliable, Multi-Modal Presentations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09804)
*Eric Xie,Danielle Waterfield,Michael Kennedy,Aidong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SlideBot是一个多智能体框架，利用LLMs、检索、结构化规划和代码生成来自动化教育演示文稿的创建，解决了现有LLM在多模态内容生成方面的不足，并通过结合认知理论和教师反馈，提高了内容的准确性、清晰度和教学价值。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SlideBot是一个模块化的多智能体框架，整合了LLMs与检索、结构化规划和代码生成。其核心支柱包括：信息性（确保内容深入且上下文相关）、可靠性（通过检索整合外部信息）和实用性（通过与教师协作实现定制和迭代反馈）。该框架借鉴了认知负荷理论（CLT）和多媒体学习认知理论（CTML）的循证教学设计原则，利用结构化规划管理内在负荷，并使用一致的视觉宏来降低外在负荷，增强双通道学习。具体而言，专门的智能体协同完成信息检索、内容摘要、图表生成和使用LaTeX格式化幻灯片，并通过交互式优化与教师的偏好保持一致。

Result: 在AI和生物医学教育领域的领域专家和学生的评估显示，SlideBot在概念准确性、清晰度和教学价值方面均表现出持续的提升。与现有方法相比，SlideBot生成的幻灯片在信息深度、相关性和教学有效性方面均有显著优势。

Conclusion: SlideBot成功地解决了LLMs在教育演示文稿生成方面面临的挑战，通过其多智能体协同框架和对认知学习理论的应用，显著提高了输出内容的准确性、相关性和教学质量。该研究证明了SlideBot在高等教育中简化幻灯片准备工作，同时确保准确性、相关性和适应性的潜力。未来的工作可以探索SlideBot在更多学科领域的应用，以及进一步优化其与教师的交互和反馈机制。

However, generating effective presentation slides introduces unique challenges due to the complexity of multimodal content creation and the need for precise, domain-specific information. Existing LLM-based solutions often fail to produce reliable and informative outputs, limiting their educational value. To address these limitations, we introduce SlideBot - a modular, multi-agent slide generation framework that integrates LLMs with retrieval, structured planning, and code generation. It incorporates evidence-based instructional design principles from Cognitive Load Theory (CLT) and the Cognitive Theory of Multimedia Learning (CTML), using structured planning to manage intrinsic load and consistent visual macros to reduce extraneous load and enhance dual-channel learning. Within the system, specialized agents collaboratively retrieve information, summarize content, generate figures, and format slides using LaTeX, aligning outputs with instructor preferences through interactive refinement. Evaluations from domain experts and students in AI and biomedical education show that SlideBot consistently enhances conceptual accuracy, clarity, and instructional value. These findings demonstrate SlideBot's potential to streamline slide preparation while ensuring accuracy, relevance, and adaptability in higher education.

The system integrates thermochromic dyes with flexible heating units to induce visually dynamic adversarial patterns on clothing surfaces. In its default state, the clothing appears as an ordinary black T-shirt. Upon heating via an embedded thermal unit, hidden adversarial patterns on the fabric are activated, allowing the wearer to effectively evade detection across both visible and infrared modalities. Physical experiments demonstrate that the adversarial wearable achieves rapid texture activation within 50 seconds and maintains an adversarial success rate above 80\% across diverse real-world surveillance environments. This work demonstrates a new pathway toward physically grounded, user-controllable anti-AI systems, highlighting the growing importance of proactive adversarial techniques for privacy protection in the age of ubiquitous AI surveillance.

### [100] [EgoEMS: A High-Fidelity Multimodal Egocentric Dataset for Cognitive Assistance in Emergency Medical Services](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09894)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究人员开发了一个开源、低成本的数据收集系统，并与EMS专家合作，收集了超过20小时的程序性EMS活动数据。该数据集从以自我为中心的视角捕捉，包含了62名参与者（包括46名EMS专业人员）在233个模拟紧急场景中的表现。数据经过详细标注，包括关键步骤、带说话人区分的音频转录、动作质量指标以及带有分割掩码的边界框。此外，还建立了一套用于实时多模态关键步骤识别和动作质量评估的基准测试。

Result: 研究提出了EgoEMS数据集，该数据集具有高保真度、多模态和多人物的特点，能够反映真实的EMS动态，包括急救人员与患者的互动。数据集的标注内容丰富，为AI模型提供了详细的学习依据。此外，研究提出的基准测试为评估AI支持工具的性能提供了量化指标，为未来的研究奠定了基础。

Conclusion: EgoEMS数据集的创建是AI在EMS领域应用的重要一步，它为开发能够减轻急救人员认知负担的AI认知助手提供了关键资源。通过提供逼真的模拟场景和详细的标注，该数据集有望推动智能EMS系统的发展，最终改善患者的治疗结果。未来的工作可以集中在利用此数据集开发更先进的AI模型，以及探索其在实际EMS操作中的部署。

In pursuit of this vision, we introduce EgoEMS, the first end-to-end, high-fidelity, multimodal, multiperson dataset capturing over 20 hours of realistic, procedural EMS activities from an egocentric view in 233 simulated emergency scenarios performed by 62 participants, including 46 EMS professionals. We hope EgoEMS inspires the research community to push the boundaries of intelligent EMS systems and ultimately contribute to improved patient outcomes.

### [101] [Learning to Pose Problems: Reasoning-Driven and Solver-Adaptive Data Synthesis for Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09907)
*Yongxian Wei,Yilin Zhao,Li Shen,Xinrui Chen,Runxi Cheng,Sinan Du,Hao Yu,Gang Liu,Jiahong Yan,Chun Yuan,Dian Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 数据合成是训练大型推理模型的一种可扩展替代方案，但现有方法存在生成无差别、缺乏推理和难以平衡难度的问题。本文提出了一种能够进行推理规划和自适应难度调整的问题生成器。通过构造相关问题对并引入问题设计 CoT，生成器可以从数据中学习问题设计策略。将求解器的反馈作为奖励信号，生成器能够校准难度并生成处于求解器能力边缘的互补问题。实验表明，该方法在 10 个数学和通用推理基准上平均提升了 2.5%，并能泛化到语言和视觉-语言模型。与求解器协同进化可进一步提升 0.7% 的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数据合成方法在为大型推理模型生成训练数据时面临两大挑战：1. 无差别生成，即生成的问题要么价值低下（忽略求解器能力），要么需要复杂的流水线来平衡难度；2. 缺乏推理能力，导致生成的问题只是现有问题的浅层变体。这些问题限制了合成数据的质量和有效性，阻碍了模型性能的提升。

Method: 本文提出了一种问题生成器，该生成器通过显式推理来规划问题方向，并在合成数据前进行难度自适应。具体方法包括：1. 构造相关问题对，并利用推理模型生成的问题设计 CoT 进行数据增强，从而引导生成器学习问题设计策略。2. 将求解器对合成问题的反馈视为奖励信号，使生成器能够校准难度，并生成处于求解器能力边缘的互补问题。3. 实验在 10 个数学和通用推理基准上进行，评估了该方法在语言模型和视觉-语言模型上的泛化能力，并进行了求解器与生成器协同进化的实验。

Result: 在 10 个数学和通用推理基准上的广泛实验表明，所提出的方法实现了 2.5% 的平均性能提升，并且能够泛化到语言模型和视觉-语言模型。此外，在合成数据上训练的求解器能够为生成器的持续训练提供改进的奖励信号，实现了协同进化，带来了额外的 0.7% 性能提升。

Conclusion: 本文提出的问题生成器通过显式推理和自适应难度调整，有效解决了现有数据合成方法的局限性，能够生成高质量、高价值的训练数据，显著提升了大型推理模型的性能。该方法在多个基准上表现出优越性，并能泛化到不同模态的模型。求解器与生成器的协同进化进一步提升了性能，展示了该方法的潜力和扩展性。未来工作可探索更复杂的推理规划和更精细的难度自适应机制。

Abstract: Data synthesis for training large reasoning models offers a scalable alternative to limited, human-curated datasets, enabling the creation of high-quality data. However, existing approaches face several challenges: (i) indiscriminate generation that ignores the solver's ability and yields low-value problems, or reliance on complex data pipelines to balance problem difficulty; and (ii) a lack of reasoning in problem generation, leading to shallow problem variants. In this paper, we develop a problem generator that reasons explicitly to plan problem directions before synthesis and adapts difficulty to the solver's ability. Specifically, we construct related problem pairs and augment them with intermediate problem-design CoT produced by a reasoning model. These data bootstrap problem-design strategies from the generator. Then, we treat the solver's feedback on synthetic problems as a reward signal, enabling the generator to calibrate difficulty and produce complementary problems near the edge of the solver's competence. Extensive experiments on 10 mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks show that our method achieves an average improvement of 2.5% and generalizes to both language and vision-language models. Moreover, a solver trained on the synthesized data provides improved rewards for continued generator training, enabling co-evolution and yielding a further 0.7% performance gain. Our code will be made publicly available here.

</details>


### [102] [OIDA-QA: A Multimodal Benchmark for Analyzing the Opioid Industry Documents Archive](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09914)
*Xuan Shen,Brian Wingenroth,Zichao Wang,Jason Kuen,Wanrong Zhu,Ruiyi Zhang,Yiwei Wang,Lichun Ma,Anqi Liu,Hongfu Liu,Tong Sun,Kevin S. Hawkins,Kate Tasker,G. Caleb Alexander,Jiuxiang Gu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过构建一个包含400,000个训练文档和10,000个测试文档的大规模数据集，并从中提取文本、视觉和布局等多模态信息，开发了针对阿片类药物危机相关法律和公司文件的领域特定多模态大语言模型（LLMs）。该模型通过整合历史问答对、引入页面引用和重要性分类器，显著提高了信息提取和问答任务的准确性。

Method: 研究人员首先对原始数据集进行组织，并构建了一个包含400,000个训练文档和10,000个测试文档的基准。然后，他们从每个文档中提取丰富的多模态信息，包括文本内容、视觉元素和布局结构。基于这些信息，研究人员利用多种人工智能模型生成了360,000个训练问答对和10,000个测试问答对。在此基础上，他们开发了领域特定的多模态大语言模型（LLMs），并探索了多模态输入对任务性能的影响。为了进一步提高响应准确性，研究人员还整合了历史问答对作为上下文信息，并引入了页面引用和重要性分类器来改进信息的相关性和精确性。

Result: 初步实验结果表明，研究开发的AI助手在文档信息提取和问答任务方面取得了显著的改进。具体性能指标和与现有方法的比较未在摘要中详述，但强调了多模态输入和所引入的增强机制（如历史问答对、页面引用和重要性分类器）对提高准确性的积极作用。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个大规模的多模态数据集，并开发了领域特定的多模态大语言模型，以应对阿片类药物危机相关文件的分析挑战。这些模型在信息提取和问答任务中展现出优越性能，为理解和解决阿片类药物危机提供了新的工具和见解。研究成果（数据集和模型）已公开，以便进一步的研究和应用。未来的工作可以集中在进一步优化模型性能，扩展到更多类型的文件，以及探索这些模型在公共卫生政策制定中的实际应用。

Abstract: The opioid crisis represents a significant moment in public health that reveals systemic shortcomings across regulatory systems, healthcare practices, corporate governance, and public policy. Analyzing how these interconnected systems simultaneously failed to protect public health requires innovative analytic approaches for exploring the vast amounts of data and documents disclosed in the UCSF-JHU Opioid Industry Documents Archive (OIDA). The complexity, multimodal nature, and specialized characteristics of these healthcare-related legal and corporate documents necessitate more advanced methods and models tailored to specific data types and detailed annotations, ensuring the precision and professionalism in the analysis. In this paper, we tackle this challenge by organizing the original dataset according to document attributes and constructing a benchmark with 400k training documents and 10k for testing. From each document, we extract rich multimodal information-including textual content, visual elements, and layout structures-to capture a comprehensive range of features. Using multiple AI models, we then generate a large-scale dataset comprising 360k training QA pairs and 10k testing QA pairs. Building on this foundation, we develop domain-specific multimodal Large Language Models (LLMs) and explore the impact of multimodal inputs on task performance. To further enhance response accuracy, we incorporate historical QA pairs as contextual grounding for answering current queries. Additionally, we incorporate page references within the answers and introduce an importance-based page classifier, further improving the precision and relevance of the information provided. Preliminary results indicate the improvements with our AI assistant in document information extraction and question-answering tasks. The dataset and models are publicly available at: https://huggingface.co/opioidarchive

### [103] [Adaptive Hyperbolic Kernels: Modulated Embedding in de Branges-Rovnyak Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.09921)
*Leping Si,Meimei Yang,Hui Xue,Shipeng Zhu,Pengfei Fang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: To address limitations in existing hyperbolic kernels for representing hierarchical data, this paper introduces an adaptive hyperbolic kernel based on a curvature-aware de Branges-Rovnyak space. This novel approach allows for adaptive selection of the appropriate reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS) corresponding to hyperbolic space with any curvature, outperforming existing methods in modeling hierarchical dependencies on visual and language benchmarks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hierarchical data is prevalent in machine learning tasks like NLP, computer vision, and social network analysis. Hyperbolic space is well-suited for embedding hierarchical structures due to its negative curvature, minimizing distortion. While kernel methods can enhance hyperbolic representation capacity, current hyperbolic kernels exhibit geometric distortion or lack adaptability. This research aims to overcome these limitations by developing more effective and adaptive hyperbolic kernels.

Method: The paper proposes a novel approach using a curvature-aware de Branges-Rovnyak space, which is a reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS) isometric to a Poincare ball. An adjustable multiplier is introduced to adaptively select the appropriate RKHS for hyperbolic spaces of any curvature. Based on this, a family of adaptive hyperbolic kernels is constructed, including a new adaptive hyperbolic radial kernel. This kernel features learnable parameters that modulate hyperbolic features in a task-aware manner. The effectiveness of these proposed kernels was evaluated through extensive experiments on visual and language benchmarks.

Result: Extensive experiments conducted on visual and language benchmarks demonstrated that the proposed adaptive hyperbolic kernels significantly outperform existing hyperbolic kernels in accurately modeling hierarchical dependencies. The results highlight the superior performance of the novel adaptive hyperbolic radial kernel and the general effectiveness of the adaptive approach in capturing complex hierarchical structures.

Conclusion: This paper successfully introduces adaptive hyperbolic kernels by leveraging a curvature-aware de Branges-Rovnyak space. The proposed method addresses the limitations of existing hyperbolic kernels by offering adaptability to curvature and task-specific feature modulation. The experimental results confirm the superiority of the new kernels in modeling hierarchical data across different domains. Future work could explore further extensions and applications of these adaptive hyperbolic kernels.

Abstract: Hierarchical data pervades diverse machine learning applications, including natural language processing, computer vision, and social network analysis. Hyperbolic space, characterized by its negative curvature, has demonstrated strong potential in such tasks due to its capacity to embed hierarchical structures with minimal distortion. Previous evidence indicates that the hyperbolic representation capacity can be further enhanced through kernel methods. However, existing hyperbolic kernels still suffer from mild geometric distortion or lack adaptability. This paper addresses these issues by introducing a curvature-aware de Branges-Rovnyak space, a reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS) that is isometric to a Poincare ball. We design an adjustable multiplier to select the appropriate RKHS corresponding to the hyperbolic space with any curvature adaptively. Building on this foundation, we further construct a family of adaptive hyperbolic kernels, including the novel adaptive hyperbolic radial kernel, whose learnable parameters modulate hyperbolic features in a task-aware manner. Extensive experiments on visual and language benchmarks demonstrate that our proposed kernels outperform existing hyperbolic kernels in modeling hierarchical dependencies.

</details>


### [104] [ChEmREF: Evaluating Language Model Readiness for Chemical Emergency Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10027)
*Risha Surana,Qinyuan Ye,Swabha Swayamdipta*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究旨在评估大型语言模型在处理危险品（HAZMAT）事件中的潜力，通过引入ChEmREF基准测试，涵盖化学品信息转换、应急响应生成和领域知识问答三个任务。研究发现，尽管语言模型在某些任务上表现出潜力，但准确率仍有待提高，且需要人类监督。

Method: 本研究引入了一个名为ChEmREF（Chemical Emergency Response Evaluation Framework）的新基准测试。ChEmREF包含1,035种HAZMAT化学品的信息，数据来源于《应急响应指南》（ERG）和PubChem数据库。该基准测试被组织成三个任务：（1）化学品表示的结构化与非结构化形式之间的转换（例如，将C2H6O转换为乙醇）；（2）应急响应生成（例如，推荐适当的疏散距离）；（3）来自化学品安全和认证考试的领域知识问答。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，大型语言模型在辅助应急响应人员执行各种任务方面显示出潜力，但由于其当前的局限性，需要进行仔细的人工监督。模型在化学品信息转换、响应建议和领域知识问答方面均取得了一定进展，但离实际应用仍有距离，未来需要进一步改进模型的准确性和可靠性。

Abstract: Emergency responders managing hazardous material HAZMAT incidents face critical, time-sensitive decisions, manually navigating extensive chemical guidelines. We investigate whether today's language models can assist responders by rapidly and reliably understanding critical information, identifying hazards, and providing recommendations.We introduce the Chemical Emergency Response Evaluation Framework (ChEmREF), a new benchmark comprising questions on 1,035 HAZMAT chemicals from the Emergency Response Guidebook and the PubChem Database. ChEmREF is organized into three tasks: (1) translation of chemical representation between structured and unstructured forms (e.g., converting C2H6O to ethanol), (2) emergency response generation (e.g., recommending appropriate evacuation distances) and (3) domain knowledge question answering from chemical safety and certification exams. Our best evaluated models received an exact match of 68.0% on unstructured HAZMAT chemical representation translation, a LLM Judge score of 52.7% on incident response recommendations, and a multiple-choice accuracy of 63.9% on HAMZAT examinations.These findings suggest that while language models show potential to assist emergency responders in various tasks, they require careful human oversight due to their current limitations.

### [105] [Beyond ReAct: A Planner-Centric Framework for Complex Tool-Augmented LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10037)
*Xiaolong Wei,Yuehu Dong,Xingliang Wang,Xingyu Zhang,Zhejun Zhao,Dongdong Shen,Long Xia,Dawei Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 现有的工具增强大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理复杂查询时面临严峻挑战，容易陷入局部优化陷阱。本文提出了一种新颖的以规划者为中心的“规划-执行”范式，通过全局有向无环图（DAG）规划来解决局部优化瓶颈。同时引入了包含复杂查询的大规模基准数据集ComplexTool-Plan，并采用监督微调（SFT）与组相对策略优化（GRPO）相结合的两阶段训练方法。该框架在StableToolBench基准测试中取得了最先进的性能，证明了其在处理复杂的多工具协同工作流方面的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的工具增强大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理复杂查询时，由于依赖增量决策过程，容易陷入局部优化陷阱。这限制了它们在需要复杂多工具协同的场景下的性能。本文旨在解决这一问题，通过引入新的范式和方法来克服这些局限性。

Method: 本文提出了一种以规划者为中心的“规划-执行”范式。核心是一个新的规划者模型，它对复杂查询执行全局有向无环图（DAG）规划。引入了大规模基准数据集ComplexTool-Plan。采用监督微调（SFT）和组相对策略优化（GRPO）的两阶段训练方法来提高规划器的准确性和全局规划意识。将该框架与执行器结合，并在StableToolBench基准测试中进行评估。

Result: 在StableToolBench基准测试中，本文提出的框架在处理复杂用户查询方面取得了最先进的性能。实验证明，该框架在端到端执行能力和处理复杂的多工具工作流方面表现出色，超越了现有方法。

Abstract: Existing tool-augmented large language models (LLMs) encounter significant challenges when processing complex queries. Current frameworks such as ReAct are prone to local optimization traps due to their reliance on incremental decision-making processes. To address these limitations, we propose a novel Planner-centric Plan-Execute paradigm that fundamentally resolves local optimization bottlenecks through architectural innovation. Central to our approach is a novel Planner model that performs global Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) planning for complex queries, enabling optimized execution beyond conventional tool coordination. We also introduce ComplexTool-Plan, a large-scale benchmark dataset featuring complex queries that demand sophisticated multi-tool composition and coordination capabilities. Additionally, we develop a two-stage training methodology that integrates Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), systematically enhancing the Planner's tool selection accuracy and global planning awareness through structured DAG-based planning. When integrated with a capable executor, our framework achieves state-of-the-art performance on the StableToolBench benchmark for complex user queries, demonstrating superior end-to-end execution capabilities and robust handling of intricate multi-tool workflows.

### [106] [Efficient Thought Space Exploration through Strategic Intervention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10038)
*Ziheng Li,Hengyi Cai,Xiaochi Wei,Yuchen Li,Shuaiqiang Wang,Zhi-Hong Deng,Dawei Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“Hint-Practice Reasoning”（HPR）的新型推理框架，通过结合大型语言模型（LLM）的指导和高效的小型模型的执行，显著提高了LLM推理的效率和准确性。HPR框架的核心在于“分布不一致性减少”（DIR）机制，它能动态识别关键的决策点，并根据大型模型提供的概率信息来优化推理路径，从而在解码更少token的情况下，也能达到甚至超越现有最先进的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型（LLM）在推理方面展现出潜力，但现有的推理扩展方法（如穷举采样）计算成本过高。研究发现，LLM在生成下一个词元（token）时，大部分预测与正确输出一致，只有少数关键词元的预测偏差会导致最终结果的错误。因此，需要一种更高效的方法来解决LLM推理成本高和准确性问题。

Method: 研究者提出了Hint-Practice Reasoning（HPR）框架，包含两个核心组件：1）“提示者”（hinter），一个强大的LLM，在关键决策点提供概率指导；2）“实践者”（practitioner），一个高效的小型模型，负责执行主要的推理步骤。HPR框架的关键创新在于“分布不一致性减少”（DIR）机制。DIR通过在树状概率空间中量化实践者推理轨迹与提示者预期分布之间的差异，动态识别需要干预的节点。该机制通过迭代更新树结构，对有希望的推理路径进行重分配权重，同时降低低概率分支的优先级。实验在算术和常识推理基准上进行了评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，HPR框架在效率和准确性之间取得了先进的权衡。在解码仅为现有方法1/5的token量时，HPR达到了与self-consistency和MCTS基线相当的性能。此外，在保持相似或更低的计算量（FLOPs）的情况下，HPR的准确率比现有方法最高提升了5.1%。

Conclusion: HPR框架通过结合大型模型指导和小型模型执行，并引入DIR机制来优化推理过程，有效解决了LLM推理成本高和准确性问题。该方法在多个推理任务上展示了优越的效率-准确性平衡，显著减少了计算开销，同时保持了高水平的性能。未来的工作可以进一步探索DIR机制的鲁棒性，以及将HPR框架应用于更广泛的推理任务和模型架构。

Abstract: While large language models (LLMs) demonstrate emerging reasoning capabilities, current inference-time expansion methods incur prohibitive computational costs by exhaustive sampling. Through analyzing decoding trajectories, we observe that most next-token predictions align well with the golden output, except for a few critical tokens that lead to deviations. Inspired by this phenomenon, we propose a novel Hint-Practice Reasoning (HPR) framework that operationalizes this insight through two synergistic components: 1) a hinter (powerful LLM) that provides probabilistic guidance at critical decision points, and 2) a practitioner (efficient smaller model) that executes major reasoning steps. The framework's core innovation lies in Distributional Inconsistency Reduction (DIR), a theoretically-grounded metric that dynamically identifies intervention points by quantifying the divergence between practitioner's reasoning trajectory and hinter's expected distribution in a tree-structured probabilistic space. Through iterative tree updates guided by DIR, HPR reweights promising reasoning paths while deprioritizing low-probability branches. Experiments across arithmetic and commonsense reasoning benchmarks demonstrate HPR's state-of-the-art efficiency-accuracy tradeoffs: it achieves comparable performance to self-consistency and MCTS baselines while decoding only 1/5 tokens, and outperforms existing methods by at most 5.1% absolute accuracy while maintaining similar or lower FLOPs.

</details>


### [107] [Radiology Workflow-Guided Hierarchical Reinforcement Fine-Tuning for Medical Report Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10065)
*Bodong Du,Honglong Yang,Xiaomeng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RadFlow是一个新提出的用于医学报告生成的框架，它通过模拟放射科医生在撰写诊断报告时的结构化工作流程，解决了现有模型忽视报告层级结构导致的不一致性问题。该框架引入了一个分层的、临床验证的奖励机制，同时考虑了报告的语言流畅性、医学准确性、影像发现与印象之间的一致性，以及印象部分的质量。此外，它还包含一个关键信息感知策略优化机制，用于处理高风险或临床敏感病例。实验证明，RadFlow在胸部X光和颈动脉超声数据集上显著提高了诊断一致性和报告的整体质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的医学报告生成（MRG）系统通常将报告视为单一序列，忽略了放射科医生在诊断过程中描述发现、总结印象并仔细斟酌关键信息的结构化工作流程。这种简化的处理方式导致生成报告在描述性内容和诊断性内容之间存在不一致性，未能充分模拟真实世界的报告撰写实践。因此，有必要开发能够体现报告层级结构和放射科医生工作流程的MRG系统，以提高报告的临床准确性和一致性。

Method: RadFlow框架通过以下方式模拟结构化报告流程：1. **层级工作流引导**：明确建模临床报告的结构化本质。2. **临床验证的奖励层级**：引入与放射科报告组织结构相呼应的奖励层级。全局奖励整合了语言流畅性、医学领域正确性以及影像发现（Finding）与印象（Impression）之间的一致性，旨在促进连贯且临床上忠实的叙述。局部奖励则侧重于印象部分的质量，强调其在诊断准确性中的核心作用。3. **关键信息感知策略优化**：该机制能够自适应地正则化学习过程，特别关注高风险或临床敏感病例，模仿放射科医生在记录关键发现时的审慎斟酌行为。通过这些组件，将结构化报告范式融入强化微调过程。实验部分使用了胸部X光和颈动脉超声数据集进行评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，RadFlow框架在胸部X光和颈动脉超声数据集上均表现出色。与最先进的基线模型相比，RadFlow在生成报告时，显著提高了诊断一致性和报告的整体质量。具体来说，该框架成功地使模型的行为与真实世界的报告实践相匹配，生成了在语言上一致且在临床上更准确的报告。

Conclusion: RadFlow通过引入一个层级化的、受临床报告结构启发的奖励机制和关键信息感知策略优化，成功地解决了现有医学报告生成系统忽略报告层级结构的问题。该框架通过模仿放射科医生的结构化工作流程，能够生成在语言流畅性、医学准确性和临床一致性方面均有显著提升的报告。实验证明了RadFlow在提高诊断一致性和整体报告质量方面的有效性，为开发更智能、更符合临床实践的医学报告生成系统提供了有前景的方向。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的报告结构和更精细的奖励函数设计。

Abstract: Radiologists compose diagnostic reports through a structured workflow: they describe visual findings, summarize them into impressions, and carefully refine statements in clinically critical cases. However, most existing medical report generation (MRG) systems treat reports as flat sequences, overlooking this hierarchical organization and leading to inconsistencies between descriptive and diagnostic content. To align model behavior with real-world reporting practices, we propose RadFlow, a hierarchical workflow-guided reinforcement optimization framework that explicitly models the structured nature of clinical reporting. RadFlow introduces a clinically grounded reward hierarchy that mirrors the organization of radiological reports. At the global level, the reward integrates linguistic fluency, medical-domain correctness, and cross-sectional consistency between Finding and Impression, promoting coherent and clinically faithful narratives. At the local level, a section-specific reward emphasizes Impression quality, reflecting its central role in diagnostic accuracy. Furthermore, a critical-aware policy optimization mechanism adaptively regularizes learning for high-risk or clinically sensitive cases, emulating the cautious refinement behavior of radiologists when documenting critical findings. Together, these components translate the structured reporting paradigm into the reinforcement fine-tuning process, enabling the model to generate reports that are both linguistically consistent and clinically aligned. Experiments on chest X-ray and carotid ultrasound datasets demonstrate that RadFlow consistently improves diagnostic coherence and overall report quality compared with state-of-the-art baselines.

### [108] [Enhancing the Medical Context-Awareness Ability of LLMs via Multifaceted Self-Refinement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10067)
*Yuxuan Zhou,Yubin Wang,Bin Wang,Chen Ning,Xien Liu,Ji Wu,Jianye Hao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在医学领域展现出巨大潜力，但在需要强上下文感知能力以提供安全、有用且符合情境的响应的真实医疗场景中表现不佳。为解决此问题，本文提出了多方面自我改进（MuSeR）方法，通过三个关键方面（决策、沟通、安全）的自我评估和改进来增强LLMs的上下文感知能力。实验结果表明，MuSeR显著提升了LLMs在HealthBench数据集上的表现，尤其是在上下文感知方面。结合知识蒸馏，一个较小的LLM（Qwen3-32B）性能超越了其教师模型，在HealthBench及其困难子集上达到了新的SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实医疗场景需要LLMs具备更强的上下文感知能力，例如识别缺失的关键信息（用户身份、病史、风险因素等），并提供安全、有用且符合情境的响应。然而，目前的LLMs在此方面表现不足，限制了它们在医疗领域的实际应用。

Method: 本文提出了多方面自我改进（MuSeR）方法，这是一个数据驱动的途径，旨在通过自我评估和改进来增强LLMs的上下文感知能力。具体来说，首先设计了一个属性条件查询生成器，通过改变角色、地理区域、意图和信息模糊程度等属性来模拟多样化的真实用户情境。然后，LLM对这些查询进行响应，并根据三个关键方面（决策、沟通、安全）进行自我评估和改进。最后，利用生成的查询和改进后的响应进行监督微调，以加强模型的上下文感知能力。此外，通过结合知识蒸馏，可以进一步提升模型性能。

Result: 在最新的HealthBench数据集上的评估结果表明，MuSeR方法显著提升了LLMs在多个方面的性能，尤其在上下文感知能力方面取得了显著进步。通过结合知识蒸馏，一个较小的LLM（Qwen3-32B）的性能超越了其教师模型，并在HealthBench数据集及其困难子集上分别取得了63.8%和43.1%的准确率，创下了所有开源LLMs在HealthBench上的新SOTA（State-of-the-Art）。

Conclusion: MuSeR方法有效地增强了LLMs在医疗领域的上下文感知能力，解决了真实医疗场景中LLMs面临的关键挑战。通过自我评估和多方面的改进，以及结合知识蒸馏，即使是较小的模型也能达到领先的性能。未来的工作可以探索更广泛的应用场景，并进一步优化改进机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown great promise in the medical domain, achieving strong performance on several benchmarks. However, they continue to underperform in real-world medical scenarios, which often demand stronger context-awareness, i.e., the ability to recognize missing or critical details (e.g., user identity, medical history, risk factors) and provide safe, helpful, and contextually appropriate responses. To address this issue, we propose Multifaceted Self-Refinement (MuSeR), a data-driven approach that enhances LLMs' context-awareness along three key facets (decision-making, communication, and safety) through self-evaluation and refinement. Specifically, we first design a attribute-conditioned query generator that simulates diverse real-world user contexts by varying attributes such as role, geographic region, intent, and degree of information ambiguity. An LLM then responds to these queries, self-evaluates its answers along three key facets, and refines its responses to better align with the requirements of each facet. Finally, the queries and refined responses are used for supervised fine-tuning to reinforce the model's context-awareness ability. Evaluation results on the latest HealthBench dataset demonstrate that our method significantly improves LLM performance across multiple aspects, with particularly notable gains in the context-awareness axis. Furthermore, by incorporating knowledge distillation with the proposed method, the performance of a smaller backbone LLM (e.g., Qwen3-32B) surpasses its teacher model, achieving a new SOTA across all open-source LLMs on HealthBench (63.8%) and its hard subset (43.1%). Code and dataset will be released at https://muser-llm.github.io.
